role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-jobpost-multi-api created Name: anihpj-jobpost-multi-api Labels: app=anihpj model=JobPost scope=multi-api service=jobpost Annotations: PolicyRule: Resources Non-Resource URLs Resource Names Verbs --------- ----------------- -------------- ----- configmaps [] [] [get list watch] deployments.apps [] [] [get list watch] deployments.extensions [] [] [get list watch] pods [] [] [get list watch] services [] [] [get list watch] cronjobs.batch [] [] [get list watch create update patch delete] jobs.batch [] [] [get list watch create update patch delete] horizontalpodautoscalers.autoscaling [] [] [get list create update]

RoleList

RoleList is a collection of Roles.

YAML Structure

apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: RoleList
metadata:
  resourceVersion: "12345"
items:
- apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
  kind: Role
  metadata:
    name: anihpj-skills-manager
    namespace: anihpj-production
  rules:
  - apiGroups: [""]
    resources: ["pods", "configmaps"]
    verbs: ["get", "list", "watch"]
- apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
  kind: Role
  metadata:
    name: anihpj-user-reader
    namespace: anihpj-production
  rules:
  - apiGroups: [""]
    resources: ["secrets"]
    verbs: ["get"]

Parameters Description

  • apiVersion: string - API version, always "rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1" for RoleList
  • kind: string - Resource type, always "RoleList"
  • metadata (ListMeta): Standard list metadata including resourceVersion
  • items ([]Role), required: List of Role objects

Return Value

  • 200 (RoleList): OK - Request successful, RoleList returned
  • 401: Unauthorized - Authentication required

5 Practical Django Examples

Example 1: List Skills Roles

This example demonstrates listing all Roles for the Skills model service.

# List all Skills Roles
kubectl get roles -n anihpj-production -l service=skills
NAME CREATED AT anihpj-skills-manager 2024-11-10T10:30:45Z anihpj-skills-reader 2024-11-09T14:20:30Z
Example 2: List User Roles with Details

This example shows listing User model Roles with detailed output.

# List User Roles with wide output
kubectl get roles -n anihpj-shared -l model=User -o wide
NAME CREATED AT anihpj-user-reader 2024-11-10T09:15:20Z anihpj-user-admin 2024-11-08T11:45:10Z
Example 3: List Author Roles in YAML

This example illustrates listing Author model Roles in YAML format.

# Get Author RoleList as YAML
kubectl get roles -n anihpj-content -l model=Author -o yaml
apiVersion: v1 items: - apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1 kind: Role metadata: name: anihpj-author-specific namespace: anihpj-content rules: - apiGroups: [""] resources: ["configmaps"] verbs: ["get", "update"] kind: List metadata: resourceVersion: ""
Example 4: List Location Roles by Label

This example demonstrates filtering Location model Roles using label selectors.

# List Location Roles by environment label
kubectl get roles -n anihpj-development -l model=Location,environment=development
NAME CREATED AT anihpj-location-dev 2024-11-10T10:33:20Z
Example 5: List All JobPost Roles Across Namespaces

This example shows listing all JobPost model Roles across all namespaces.

# List all JobPost Roles in all namespaces
kubectl get roles --all-namespaces -l model=JobPost
NAMESPACE NAME CREATED AT anihpj-jobs anihpj-jobpost-multi-api 2024-11-10T10:35:15Z anihpj-prod anihpj-jobpost-manager 2024-11-09T16:20:40Z

Role Operations

Operations Overview

get - Read the specified Role
list - List Roles in namespace
list all - List Roles in all namespaces
create - Create a Role
update - Replace the specified Role
patch - Partially update the specified Role
delete - Delete a Role
deletecollection - Delete collection of Roles

Operations allow you to interact with Role resources through the Kubernetes API. These operations enable you to manage authorization policies for your anihpj Django application, ensuring proper access control to cluster resources within namespaces.

get - read the specified Role

Read details of a specific Role by name within a namespace.

HTTP Request
GET /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles/{name}
Parameters
  • name (in path): string, required - name of the Role
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace of the Role
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
Return Value
  • 200 (Role): OK
  • 401: Unauthorized
5 Practical Django Examples
Example 1: Get Skills Role Details

This example demonstrates retrieving details of the Skills model Role.

# Get Skills Role
kubectl get role anihpj-skills-manager -n anihpj-production -o yaml
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1 kind: Role metadata: name: anihpj-skills-manager namespace: anihpj-production labels: app: anihpj model: Skills rules: - apiGroups: [""] resources: ["pods", "configmaps", "secrets"] verbs: ["get", "list", "watch", "create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
Example 2: Get User Role with Rules

This example shows retrieving User Role with detailed rules information.

# Get User Role details
kubectl describe role anihpj-user-reader -n anihpj-shared
Name: anihpj-user-reader Labels: app=anihpj model=User permission=readonly Annotations: PolicyRule: Resources Non-Resource URLs Resource Names Verbs --------- ----------------- -------------- ----- configmaps [] [] [get list watch] secrets [] [] [get list watch]
Example 3: Get Author Role JSON

This example illustrates retrieving Author Role in JSON format.

# Get Author Role as JSON
kubectl get role anihpj-author-specific -n anihpj-content -o json
{ "apiVersion": "rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1", "kind": "Role", "metadata": { "name": "anihpj-author-specific", "namespace": "anihpj-content", "labels": { "app": "anihpj", "model": "Author" } }, "rules": [ { "apiGroups": [""], "resources": ["configmaps"], "resourceNames": ["anihpj-author-config"], "verbs": ["get", "update"] } ] }
Example 4: Get Location Role Custom Output

This example demonstrates retrieving Location Role with custom columns.

# Get Location Role with custom output
kubectl get role anihpj-location-dev -n anihpj-development -o custom-columns=NAME:.metadata.name,NAMESPACE:.metadata.namespace,CREATED:.metadata.creationTimestamp
NAME NAMESPACE CREATED anihpj-location-dev anihpj-development 2024-11-10T10:33:20Z
Example 5: Get JobPost Role JSONPath

This example shows retrieving specific JobPost Role fields using JSONPath.

# Get JobPost Role rules using JSONPath
kubectl get role anihpj-jobpost-multi-api -n anihpj-jobs -o jsonpath='{.rules[*].verbs}'
[get list watch] [get list watch create update patch delete] [get list create update]

list - list or watch objects of kind Role

List Roles in a specific namespace with optional filtering and pagination.

HTTP Request
GET /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles
Parameters
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace to list Roles from
  • allowWatchBookmarks (in query): boolean - allow watch bookmarks
  • continue (in query): string - continue token for pagination
  • fieldSelector (in query): string - field selector to filter results
  • labelSelector (in query): string - label selector to filter results
  • limit (in query): integer - maximum number of results
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
  • resourceVersion (in query): string - resource version
  • resourceVersionMatch (in query): string - how to match resource version
  • sendInitialEvents (in query): boolean - send initial events
  • timeoutSeconds (in query): integer - timeout in seconds
  • watch (in query): boolean - watch for changes
Return Value
  • 200 (RoleList): OK
  • 401: Unauthorized

list - list or watch objects of kind Role (All Namespaces)

List Roles across all namespaces in the cluster.

HTTP Request
GET /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/roles
Parameters
  • allowWatchBookmarks (in query): boolean - allow watch bookmarks
  • continue (in query): string - continue token for pagination
  • fieldSelector (in query): string - field selector to filter results
  • labelSelector (in query): string - label selector to filter results
  • limit (in query): integer - maximum number of results
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
  • resourceVersion (in query): string - resource version
  • resourceVersionMatch (in query): string - how to match resource version
  • sendInitialEvents (in query): boolean - send initial events
  • timeoutSeconds (in query): integer - timeout in seconds
  • watch (in query): boolean - watch for changes
Return Value
  • 200 (RoleList): OK
  • 401: Unauthorized

create - create a Role

Create a new Role in a namespace to define permissions.

HTTP Request
POST /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles
Parameters
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace to create the Role in
  • body: Role, required - Role object to create
  • dryRun (in query): string - dry run mode
  • fieldManager (in query): string - field manager name
  • fieldValidation (in query): string - field validation policy
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
Return Value
  • 200 (Role): OK
  • 201 (Role): Created
  • 202 (Role): Accepted
  • 401: Unauthorized
5 Django Create Role Examples
Example 1: Create Skills Manager Role

This example demonstrates creating a manager Role for Skills model service.

# Create Skills manager Role
kubectl create role anihpj-skills-manager --verb=get,list,watch,create,update --resource=pods,configmaps -n anihpj-production
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-skills-manager created
Example 2: Create User Reader Role from YAML

This example shows creating a readonly Role for User authentication service.

# Create User reader Role from file
kubectl create -f user-reader-role.yaml
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-user-reader created
Example 3: Create Author Specific Role with Dry Run

This example illustrates creating an Author Role with dry run validation.

# Create Author Role with dry run
kubectl create -f author-specific-role.yaml --dry-run=client -o yaml
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1 kind: Role metadata: name: anihpj-author-specific namespace: anihpj-content rules: - apiGroups: [""] resources: ["configmaps"] resourceNames: ["anihpj-author-config"] verbs: ["get", "update"]
Example 4: Create Location Development Role

This example demonstrates creating a comprehensive development Role for Location service.

# Create Location development Role
kubectl create role anihpj-location-dev --verb=* --resource=* -n anihpj-development
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-location-dev created
Example 5: Create JobPost Multi-API Role

This example shows creating a multi-API group Role for JobPost operations.

# Create JobPost multi-API Role from file
kubectl apply -f jobpost-multi-api-role.yaml
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-jobpost-multi-api created

update - replace the specified Role

Replace an existing Role with a new definition.

HTTP Request
PUT /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles/{name}
Parameters
  • name (in path): string, required - name of the Role
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace of the Role
  • body: Role, required - updated Role object
  • dryRun (in query): string - dry run mode
  • fieldManager (in query): string - field manager name
  • fieldValidation (in query): string - field validation policy
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
Return Value
  • 200 (Role): OK
  • 201 (Role): Created
  • 401: Unauthorized
5 Django Update Role Examples
Example 1: Update Skills Role Permissions

This example demonstrates updating Skills Role to add delete permission.

# Update Skills Role from file
kubectl apply -f skills-manager-role-updated.yaml
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-skills-manager configured

role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-jobpost-multi-api configured

patch - partially update the specified Role

Partially update a Role without replacing the entire object.

HTTP Request
PATCH /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles/{name}
Parameters
  • name (in path): string, required - name of the Role
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace of the Role
  • body: Patch, required - patch data
  • dryRun (in query): string - dry run mode
  • fieldManager (in query): string - field manager name
  • fieldValidation (in query): string - field validation policy
  • force (in query): boolean - force update
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
Return Value
  • 200 (Role): OK
  • 201 (Role): Created
  • 401: Unauthorized
5 Django Patch Role Examples
Example 1: Patch Skills Role Labels

This example demonstrates patching Skills Role to add new labels.

# Patch Skills Role labels
kubectl patch role anihpj-skills-manager -n anihpj-production --type merge -p '{"metadata":{"labels":{"version":"v2"}}}'
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-skills-manager patched
Example 2: Patch User Role Add Verb

This example shows patching User Role to add a new verb to existing rules.

# Patch User Role to add delete verb
kubectl patch role anihpj-user-reader -n anihpj-shared --type json -p='[{"op":"add","path":"/rules/0/verbs/-","value":"delete"}]'
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-user-reader patched
Example 3: Patch Author Role Annotations

This example illustrates patching Author Role to update annotations.

# Patch Author Role annotations
kubectl patch role anihpj-author-specific -n anihpj-content -p '{"metadata":{"annotations":{"description":"Updated author permissions"}}}'
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-author-specific patched
Example 4: Patch Location Role Add Resource

This example demonstrates patching Location Role to include additional resources.

# Patch Location Role to add resource
kubectl patch role anihpj-location-dev -n anihpj-development --type json -p='[{"op":"add","path":"/rules/0/resources/-","value":"services"}]'
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-location-dev patched
Example 5: Patch JobPost Role Add Rule

This example shows patching JobPost Role to add a completely new rule.

# Patch JobPost Role to add new rule
kubectl patch role anihpj-jobpost-multi-api -n anihpj-jobs --type json -p='[{"op":"add","path":"/rules/-","value":{"apiGroups":["networking.k8s.io"],"resources":["ingresses"],"verbs":["get","list"]}}]'
role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io/anihpj-jobpost-multi-api patched

delete - delete a Role

Delete a specific Role from a namespace.

HTTP Request
DELETE /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles/{name}
Parameters
  • name (in path): string, required - name of the Role
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace of the Role
  • body: DeleteOptions - delete options
  • dryRun (in query): string - dry run mode
  • gracePeriodSeconds (in query): integer - grace period in seconds
  • ignoreStoreReadErrorWithClusterBreakingPotential (in query): boolean - ignore store read errors
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
  • propagationPolicy (in query): string - propagation policy
Return Value
  • 200 (Status): OK
  • 202 (Status): Accepted
  • 401: Unauthorized

This example demonstrates deleting a temporary Skills development Role.

role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io "anihpj-jobpost-v1" deleted

deletecollection - delete collection of Role

Delete multiple Roles matching label selector criteria.

HTTP Request
DELETE /apis/rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1/namespaces/{namespace}/roles
Parameters
  • namespace (in path): string, required - namespace to delete Roles from
  • body: DeleteOptions - delete options
  • continue (in query): string - continue token
  • dryRun (in query): string - dry run mode
  • fieldSelector (in query): string - field selector
  • gracePeriodSeconds (in query): integer - grace period in seconds
  • ignoreStoreReadErrorWithClusterBreakingPotential (in query): boolean - ignore store read errors
  • labelSelector (in query): string - label selector
  • limit (in query): integer - limit
  • pretty (in query): string - pretty print output
  • propagationPolicy (in query): string - propagation policy
  • resourceVersion (in query): string - resource version
  • resourceVersionMatch (in query): string - resource version match
  • sendInitialEvents (in query): boolean - send initial events
  • timeoutSeconds (in query): integer - timeout in seconds
Return Value
  • 200 (Status): OK
  • 401: Unauthorized
5 Django Collection Delete Examples
Example 1: Delete All Skills Test Roles

This example demonstrates deleting all Skills test Roles using label selector.

# Delete all Skills test Roles
kubectl delete roles -n anihpj-development -l model=Skills,environment=test

Example 2: Delete All User Development Roles

This example shows deleting all User development Roles with dry run.

role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io "anihpj-user-dev-1" deleted (dry run) role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io "anihpj-user-dev-2" deleted (dry run)
Example 3: Delete All Author Temporary Roles

This example illustrates deleting temporary Author Roles based on tier label.

Example 4: Delete All Location Old Version Roles

This example demonstrates deleting old version Location Roles during upgrade.

Example 5: Delete All JobPost Non-Production Roles

This example shows deleting all non-production JobPost Roles.

# List what would be deleted
kubectl get roles -n anihpj-jobs -l model=JobPost,environment!=production
# Delete non-production JobPost Roles
kubectl delete roles -n anihpj-jobs -l model=JobPost,environment!=production
NAME AGE anihpj-jobpost-dev 2d anihpj-jobpost-staging 1d role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io "anihpj-jobpost-dev" deleted role.rbac.authorization.k8s.io "anihpj-jobpost-staging" deleted
